<h4><strong>Ease of Use</strong></h4>
<p></p> I’ll be straightforward: Duda isn’t the easiest-to-use website builder. However, when a builder ranks low in our ease of use category, it’s usually due to poor design, a clunky user interface, or confusing navigation. Duda doesn’t really suffer from any of those problems. In fact, <strong>the Duda editor is responsive, clear, and easy to navigate –</strong> it’s just not designed with the average user in mind. 
<p></p> Duda proudly targets its products to more experienced designers. That means you get access to a (very) wide variety of tools that, while useful, can quickly get overwhelming if you don’t already have a web design background. Duda does provide learning resources through “Duda University,” a comprehensive knowledge base for teaching important aspects about how Duda and web design work. But even then, <strong>the</strong><strong> learning curve can be pretty steep.</strong> 
<figure id="attachment_3196744" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3196744"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:55.625% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/image-issue-8.png"  width="1600" height="890" alt="Duda Flex Designn." /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/image-issue-8.png"   width="1600" height="890" alt="Duda Flex Designn." class="border wp-image-3196744 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3196744"class="wp-caption-text">Duda is a very intuitive builder if you’re an experienced designer.</figcaption></figure> That said, if you do have the required experience, Duda is one of the easiest website builders<strong> on that level</strong><strong>.</strong> The interface uses a mix of drag-and-drop building and CSS editing that works just right. Duda’s editor is neatly organized, and it gives you full design control, from the overall site appearance down to the specific details. 
<h4><strong>Design Flexibility</strong></h4>
<p></p> <strong>Duda’s editor combines the classic drag-and-drop style of building with CSS editing to give you full control over how your site looks.</strong> You can add over 60 widgets and hundreds of pre-made sections to your site for quick building, and you get virtually limitless customization over each element. 
<p></p> What really makes Duda stand out from the crowd, though, is its advanced Flex editor. Flex mode provides a visual interface for editing the CSS code of different elements. <strong>It also allows for</strong><strong> incredibly precise editing over spacing and breakpoints, which can make or break the visual quality of a website.</strong> 
<figure id="attachment_3196773" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-3196773"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:56.25% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/image-issue-9.png"  width="1600" height="900" alt="Duda Flex Sections." /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/image-issue-9.png"   width="1600" height="900" alt="Duda Flex Sections." class="border wp-image-3196773 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-3196773"class="wp-caption-text">Duda’s pre-made sections are incredibly well-designed and very customizable.</figcaption></figure> <strong>Duda also allows you to fine-tune your design for any screen size.</strong> The editor itself is mobile-responsive, so you could just edit your website for desktop and be done with it, but you can also make custom changes to ensure your website looks just right on any screen. 
<p></p> All-in-all, Duda offers an unmatched level of flexibility. If complete customization is what you want, Duda could be the builder for you. 
<h4><strong>E-commerce Features</strong></h4>
<p></p> Duda provides a very intuitive – but otherwise standard – set of e-commerce features. You can add products to categories, track shipping information, and choose from over 110 different payment providers for your site. While its e-commerce features aren’t as varied as its design features, it offers enough to run and manage an online store. 
<p></p> Keep in mind, however, that e-commerce functionalities come at an extra cost. So, if you want to turn your website into a business, you&#8217;ll have to pay a premium. 
<h4><strong>Pricing</strong></h4>
<p></p> Duda’s prices are decent. In particular, the Basic plan offers outstanding design features at a very competitive price. Not only do you unlock full access to all of Duda’s state-of-the-art design features, but you also get free lifetime Amazon AWS hosting (one of the top-quality hosting services out there) as well as free domain and email hosting for a year.

<p></p> The more expensive plans don’t add much in terms of editing features. Instead, they include attractive tools for design agencies, such as team member accounts, client billing, and backend branding options. Even though each plan upgrade comes at a reasonable cost, the custom “white label” option is where prices can really skyrocket. I wouldn’t worry too much about that, though – it’s specifically designed for enterprise-level design agencies. 
<p></p> Duda gives you plenty of room to try it out before making a long-term commitment. <strong>It</strong><strong> offers a 14-day free trial and a 30-day money-back guarantee.</strong> 
<h4><strong>Other Features</strong></h4>
<p></p> Duda packs many additional features that help you expand the functionality and reach of your site. Some of my favorites are: 
<ul>
<li><strong>Amazon Web Services hosting and content delivery network: </strong>Amazon’s AWS is used by some of the biggest builders out there. Thanks to Amazon’s infrastructure, you can be sure that you’ll receive the best possible performance and security.</li>
<li><strong>Multi-language capabilities: </strong>Duda comes with simple options to help you create multi-language versions of your site.</li>
<li><strong>Simple editor mode: </strong>If you’re designing for a client, you can deliver the finished website along with a “simple editor,” which gives them easy tools to make small changes to their site.</li>
<li><strong>Backend Branding.</strong> You can add your own company’s branding to your editor’s backend. That way, your clients will always know who helped them design the website of their dreams.</li>
</ul>

<h4>Ease of Use</h4>
<p></p> Hostinger website builder is very, very easy to use. As a complete “Hostinger newbie,” it took me less than five minutes to get to grips with the basics. One potential downside is that Hostinger doesn’t give you a helpful start-up checklist or walkthrough wizard, but it doesn’t take more than a bit of clicking and scrolling to orientate yourself. Everything is pretty intuitive. 
<p></p> That being said, since Hostinger does things slightly differently from other website builders, there were a<b> few moments where I got a little stuck</b>. Buttons, for instance, weren’t exactly where I expected them to be&#8230; but that might just be my prior experience speaking, and so not necessarily a problem for complete beginners. 
<p></p> In an attempt to make life even easier for you, Hostinger offers a <b>whole suite of AI tools</b>. If inspiration is eluding you, there’s an AI business name generator, a slogan generator, a blog title generator, and even an AI writer that will generate pages of SEO-friendly content for you. 
<p></p> The text it generated for me was definitely on the bland side &#8211; and on balance I think I’d prefer to write my own copy, thank you very much. But it could definitely help get the creative juices flowing if you’re suffering from blank page syndrome and don’t know where to start. 
<figure id="attachment_1948039" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1948039"class="wp-caption alignnone"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:46.743095362168% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Zyro-AI-Tools-e1618301566760.png"  width="1919" height="897" alt="Zyro AI Tools e1618301566760" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Zyro-AI-Tools-e1618301566760.png"   width="1919" height="897" alt="Zyro AI Tools e1618301566760" class="wp-image-1948039 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1948039"class="wp-caption-text">I’m not sure I would let the AI writer create my entire website for me, but hey, it’s there if you need it!</figcaption></figure> Overall, Hostinger&#8217;s set of features is relatively minimalist, which helps on the ease-of-use front since there isn’t a huge amount to get your head around. The downside is that <strong>Hostinger</strong> <b>might be lacking a certain feature </b>you’re looking for. 
<p></p> In my case, for instance, I wasn’t able to add a calendar or an event page. I asked the live chat support about this problem and was told I had to create a calendar with an external provider and then embed the code on my website. Not ideal. 
<h4>Design Flexibility</h4>
<p></p> For a simple website builder, <strong>Hostinger</strong> <b>actually offers a pretty decent amount of design flexibility</b>. The templates are all nicely put-together, but you’re by no means locked into the way they are designed or laid out. 
<p></p> For instance, you can choose an overall color scheme for your site to make life simple for yourself, but that doesn’t mean you’re then restricted to those colors. In fact, <b>you can edit the color of every individual element as you see fit</b>. 
<figure id="attachment_1948068" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1948068"class="wp-caption aligncenter"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:44.957537154989% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Zyro-Shop-Editor-e1668791217248.png"  width="1884" height="847" alt="Zyro setting button color" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Zyro-Shop-Editor-e1668791217248.png"   width="1884" height="847" alt="Zyro setting button color" class="border wp-image-1948068 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1948068"class="wp-caption-text">No rigid color palettes here! I like that Hostinger lets you edit individual elements</figcaption></figure> In terms of fonts, you have to set text styles for headings and paragraphs across your entire website &#8211; but that’s just good design practice, and so not necessarily a drawback. 
<p></p> It’s also easy to edit the size, placement, and order of individual elements using the drag-and-drop editor.<b> Hostinger uses a grid-based layout</b>, which means that elements snap into place on a grid as you drag and drop them around the page. 
<p></p> This can take some getting used to &#8211; a couple of times, my button or block of text suddenly flew away from where I’d placed it &#8211; but <b>overall, I liked this feature.</b> You can’t put things wherever you like (this isn’t Wix), but it’s a great way of making sure that your site stays <b>neat and well-spaced</b>. 
<h4>E-commerce Features</h4>
<p></p> <b>Hostinger ’s e-commerce features, available with the eCommerce plan upwards, are robust and easy to use</b>. You have to exit the website editor and enter the <em>Store Manager</em> to start building your website store, but navigating between the two is very simple. 
<p></p> Hostinger also gives you a helpful step-by-step list of tasks to complete to get your online store up and running. It guides you through the basic process of adding products, specifying delivery options, and setting up payments. 
<p></p> It got a little trickier when it came to categorizing my products, tracking my inventory, and creating product variants (this last part in particular had me lost in a sea of error messages for a few minutes). Of course, tricky doesn’t mean impossible, and I was able to figure it out in the end. 
<p></p> The main thing that bugged me, though, was that <strong>Hostinger</strong> <b>doesn’t have a ready-made content block for displaying featured products</b> on the homepage &#8211; a pretty standard feature on most other website builders. Instead, my only option was to insert an entire duplicate of my store page. Weird. 
<figure id="attachment_1948097" aria-describedby="caption-attachment-1948097"class="wp-caption alignnone"><span class="ll-img-wrapper "  style="padding:42.991141219385% 0 0; max-width: 850px;"><noscript><img src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Zyro-Shop-Preview-e1618301713324.png"  width="1919" height="825" alt="Zyro featured products homepage block" /></noscript><img data-src="https://dt2sdf0db8zob.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2020/06/Zyro-Shop-Preview-e1618301713324.png"   width="1919" height="825" alt="Zyro featured products homepage block" class="wp-image-1948097 size-full ll-img"/></span><figcaption id="caption-attachment-1948097"class="wp-caption-text">I really don’t understand why Hostinger doesn’t offer a featured products block!</figcaption></figure>
<h4>Pricing</h4>
<p></p> The price of Hostinger&#8217;s single premium plan is pretty cheap &#8211; and I&#8217;d say it offers great value, considering what you get. Its heavily discount if you pay annually, and it also includes a free domain name for the first year. 
<p></p> But I don’t think it would be unfair to say that<b> Hostinger is a little </b><b><i>sneaky</i></b>. For instance, the advertised price assumes you’ll pay upfront for a <i>four-year contract</i>. That’s one heck of a commitment. If you factor in the extra cost of paying monthly, you might find you get more for your money elsewhere &#8211; especially considering Hostinger’s below-average PageSpeed Insight Score. 
<p></p> It’s also frustrating that<b> there isn’t a free trial</b>, which most of Hostinger ’s competitors offer if they don’t have a free plan. Personally, I was a bit put off by the prospect of having to get my credit card out without having tested the product first. That said, Hostinger does have a 30-day money-back guarantee, so… free trial in reverse? 
<div class="pricing-vendor" ></div>
<h4>Other features</h4>
<p></p> As a relatively simple website builder, Hostinger doesn’t offer loads of extra features, but it does cover the basics and quite a bit more besides. Some of the best features on offer include: 
<ul>
<li aria-level="1">Comprehensive suite of SEO and marketing tools, including heat maps (for tracking how your users interact with your website), Facebook Pixel integration, Facebook Live Chat integration, Google Analytics, and Google Tag Manager</li>
<li aria-level="1">Dedicated mobile editor for editing desktop and mobile page layouts separately</li>
<li aria-level="1">iOS and Android mobile app for managing your online store on-the-go</li>
<li aria-level="1">Website Importer tool that can import text and images from your existing website to Hostinger</li>
</ul>
<p style="text-align: left;"><div class="shortcode-external-button-link"><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=65966&lang=en&deep_id=0&deep_name=&btn_name=ButtonExternalUrl_65966_top10_145_880335&post_id=145&pageview_id=0&direct_link=&type=top10&amp=0" data-id="65966" rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" class="clickoutLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'ButtonExternalUrl_65966_top10_145_880335', 'zyro', this,  true  );">Try Hostinger Now</a></div> 
<h3><strong> What I Learned and What Surprised Me</strong></h3>
<p></p> Before taking on this project, I hadn’t given much thought to just how different website builders can be. This testing process showed me just how much range there is, and how <strong>you truly do need the right website builder in order to have the best experience</strong> for both you as the person building the site and your visitors. 
<p></p> What surprised me the most was seeing the trade-offs of design flexibility and other factors in action. In general, website builders that offer more flexibility, like Wix, took longer to build and have slower page load speeds, while those that limit your options make the site build go faster and are more guaranteed to have good design (because you can’t mess it up by deciding your DIY layout is better). 
<p></p> After testing so many website builders and creating actual websites, here’s the main advice I’d give to those deciding on a website builder: 
<ul>
<li><strong>Know your site goals ahead of time</strong>. Do you want to sell products or run a blog? Both? This will help you pick the right website builder, as they all have different strengths. Opt for a more flexible one if you aren’t sure.</li>
<li><strong>Cheap (or free) isn’t always better</strong>. Some website builders have really great value plans, but overall, you get what you pay for. You and your visitors will have a better experience if you’re willing to pay for a plan.</li>
<li><strong>It’s okay to rely on pre-made designs</strong>. Lots of website builders want you to know you have a lot of flexibility, but doing a lot of DIY design has the potential to go poorly quickly. If you know you don’t have an eye for design, choosing a builder that has strong guidelines built-in, like Squarespace, can be really helpful.</li>
</ul> There’s a lot of personal preference that goes into choosing a website builder, so think carefully about what you need from one before committing. If you need more help in making your decision, read through our extensive reviews on each website builder for more information. 
<h2 id="hselect-4" class="">FAQ</h2>
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">Is it better to build my own website, or should I hire a web designer?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">As I learned through my website builder tests, <strong>it’s pretty simple to <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">build a website yourself</a> &#8211; even with no design experience!</strong> When you build your own website, you’ll save money on hiring a designer and can make as many changes as you like, without having to go back and forth with a designer for edits. However, building your own site may take a bit longer and be limited by the customization options of the builder you choose. 
<p></p> If you hire a designer, you’ll find yourself paying more for their time and experience (although you can <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/goto.php?id=1934&#038;lang=en&#038;deep_id=0&#038;deep_name=&#038;btn_name=VendorExternalUrl_1934_top10_145_483160&#038;post_id=145&#038;pageview_id=0&#038;direct_link=&#038;type=top10&#038;amp=0"  rel="sponsored noopener norefferer" data-id="1934" class="clickoutLink boldLink shortC" target="_blank" onclick="trackClickout('event', 'clickout', 'VendorExternalUrl_1934_top10_145_483160', 'fiverr', this,  true  );"><strong>use Fiverr to find inexpensive options</strong></a>), but you’ll get a stunning professional design that is unique to you.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What is the best free website builder?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline"><strong>Not all free website builder plans are created equal</strong> &#8211; some limit the number of pages you can build to the single digits, while others limit you only by the amount of storage space. Almost all place ads on your site. Check out our assessment of the <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/best-really-free-website-builders-tried-tested/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">best free website builders</a></strong> to see which one is best for your needs.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">How much does a website builder plan cost?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">Paid website builder plans have a wide range, depending on the level of plan and the features it offers. During this test, prices ranged for $4 for a personal plan on one builder to over $50 for a premium business plan on another. (There are also enterprise level plans that cost in the hundreds.) 
<p></p> On average, the most popular plans are between $12-$25 per month, if you purchase the annual plan. Paying for a year upfront will save you money overall, but will require a higher payment initially. 
<p></p> Don’t miss our <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/wix-pricing-plan-best/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>ultimate guide to Wix pricing</strong></a>.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">When should you upgrade to a paid website builder plan?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">You should upgrade to a paid plan as soon as you need a custom domain to start building brand and SEO authority online. Every site builder on this list requires a paid plan to connect a custom domain. With a paid plan, you’ll also typically remove built-in ads, which can also help your brand image. 
<p></p> If you don’t have a pressing need for a custom domain, upgrading to a paid plan will depend largely on your site needs and the builder you choose. As soon as your site needs to outgrow the free plan, you should upgrade &#8211; but that could be when you need more than 5 pages on Jimdo, or when you need more than 500 MB of storage on Wix.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">What is a drag-and-drop website builder?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline">A drag-and-drop website builder refers to the ability to add and move site elements anywhere on a web page, simply by clicking them with your mouse and moving them to your desired location. This is different from a block editor, which has more parameters around what you can put on your site and where.</span> 
<h3 class="shortcode-faq-question-inline">How and where should I get my domain name?</h3>
<span class="shortcode-faq-answer-inline"><strong>Most website builders will offer a free domain name with a yearlong subscription to a paid plan</strong>, which is typically the easiest option for obtaining your domain name. You can also find domain names from domain registrars or <a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/web-hosting/" target="_blank" rel="noopener"><strong>web hosting providers</strong></a>. Check out our <strong><a href="https://www.websiteplanet.com/blog/ultimate-guide-to-choosing-a-domain-name/" target="_blank" rel="noopener">guide to choosing a domain name</a></strong> if you need more help.</span><div class="videoshortcode" data-videokey="26" data-pagename="VideoEmbed-__0" data-id="1779340" data-videoname="No Hype, Just Facts: Top 10 Best Website Builders in 2023">
    <span class="ll-iframe-wrapper" style="padding:56.25% 0 0;"><noscript><iframe src="https://youtube.com/embed/yHG1fdZRDGQ?rel=0" class="" width="0" height="400"></iframe></noscript><iframe data-src="https://youtube.com/embed/yHG1fdZRDGQ?rel=0" class=" ll-fr" title="No Hype, Just Facts: Top 10 Best Website Builders in 2023"  frameborder="0" width="0" height="400" allowfullscreen></iframe></span>
</div>
